<request>
// Close days menu and extract visible result anchors
await page.keyboard.press('Escape');
const s14 = await snapshot(page, {interactive:true});
console.log(s14.diff || s14.tree);
const links1 = await page.locator('a').evaluateAll(as => as.map(a => ({text: (a.textContent||'').trim().replace(/\s+/g,' '), href: a.href})).filter(x => x.href.includes('/dog/')));
console.log(JSON.stringify(links1.slice(0,30), null, 2));

const graphQuery2 = `query SearchAnimal($pagination: PaginationInfoInput!, $sort: [SortInput!]!, $filters: AnimalSearchFiltersInput!, $facets: AnimalSearchFacetsInput) {
  searchAnimal(pagination: $pagination, sort: $sort, filters: $filters, facets: $facets, isConsumer: true) {
    totalCount
    timedOut
    animals {
      animalId animalName animalType primaryPhotoId distance matchLabel outOfTown
      publicUrl { url }
      residency { adoptionStatus adoptionDate adoptionStatusChangeDate intakeDate }
      behavior { houseTrained interactions { cats dogs otherAnimals childrenUnder8 children8AndUp } }
      organization { organizationName organizationCity organizationState organizationDisplayId }
      physical { coatLength sex species breed { primary secondary mixed } age { value label rangeLabel } size { label } }
    }
  }
}`;
const vars2 = {
  pagination: {fromPage:0, pageSize: 5},
  sort: [{point:{lat:37.5952304, lon:-122.043969, order:'ASC', unit:'mi'}}],
  filters: {adoption_status:['ADOPTABLE'], animal_type:['Dog'], cats:true, children_under_8:true, coat_length:['Short'], out_of_town:null, point:{distance:'100mi', lat:37.5952304, lon:-122.043969}, record_status:['PUBLISHED']},
  facets: {age:'', breeds:'', cats:'', children_8_and_up:'', children_under_8:'', coat_length:'', colors:'', dogs:'', house_trained:'', other_animals:'', sex:'', size:'', special_needs:''}
};
const gres2 = await fetch('https://psl.petfinder.com/graphql', {method:'POST', headers:{'content-type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({operationName:'SearchAnimal', query: graphQuery2, variables: vars2})});
const gj2 = await gres2.json().catch(async e => ({parseError: await gres2.text()}));
console.log(gres2.status + ' ' + JSON.stringify(gj2, null, 2).slice(0,5000));

[64] system_message (background-consult):
<system_message>
The UI doesn't support a 30+ days filter (max is 10 days), but you already have the GraphQL endpoint working perfectly. Go directly through the API: fetch all pages of `searchAnimal` with the current filters (cats=true, children_under_8=true, coat_length=["Short"], 100mi of 94587), retrieve each animal's `residency.intakeDate`, then filter client-side for those where `today - intakeDate > 30 days`. Page through with `fromPage` increments until you've covered all 526 results. This avoids the UI dead-end entirely.
</system_message>

const today2 = new Date('2026-05-13T18:13:33Z');
const searchQueryAll2 = `query SearchAnimal($pagination: PaginationInfoInput!, $sort: [SortInput!]!, $filters: AnimalSearchFiltersInput!, $facets: AnimalSearchFacetsInput) {
  searchAnimal(pagination: $pagination, sort: $sort, filters: $filters, facets: $facets, isConsumer: true) {
    totalCount
    timedOut
    animals {
      animalId animalName animalType distance outOfTown
      publicUrl { url }
      residency { adoptionStatus adoptionDate adoptionStatusChangeDate intakeDate }
      behavior { interactions { cats dogs otherAnimals childrenUnder8 children8AndUp } }
      organization { organizationName organizationCity organizationState organizationDisplayId }
      physical { coatLength sex species breed { primary secondary mixed } age { value label rangeLabel } size { label } }
    }
  }
}`;
const searchVarsBase2 = {
  sort: [{point:{lat:37.5952304, lon:-122.043969, order:'ASC', unit:'mi'}}],
  filters: {adoption_status:['ADOPTABLE'], animal_type:['Dog'], cats:true, children_under_8:true, coat_length:['Short'], out_of_town:null, point:{distance:'100mi', lat:37.5952304, lon:-122.043969}, record_status:['PUBLISHED']},
  facets: {age:'', breeds:'', cats:'', children_8_and_up:'', children_under_8:'', coat_length:'', colors:'', dogs:'', house_trained:'', other_animals:'', sex:'', size:'', special_needs:''}
};
async function fetchSearchPage2(fromPage, pageSize) {
  const body = {operationName:'SearchAnimal', query: searchQueryAll2, variables: {...searchVarsBase2, pagination:{fromPage, pageSize}}};
  const r = await fetch('https://psl.petfinder.com/graphql', {method:'POST', headers:{'content-type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify(body)});
  const j = await r.json();
  if (j.errors) throw new Error(JSON.stringify(j.errors));
  return j.data.searchAnimal;
}
const firstPage2 = await fetchSearchPage2(0, 100);
console.log('first total '+firstPage2.totalCount+' returned '+firstPage2.animals.length+' first names '+firstPage2.animals.slice(0,3).map(a=>a.animalName).join(', '));
const pagesNeeded2 = Math.ceil(firstPage2.totalCount / 100);
const pageResults2 = [firstPage2];
for (let i=1;i<pagesNeeded2;i++) pageResults2.push(await fetchSearchPage2(i, 100));
const allAnimals2 = pageResults2.flatMap(p => p.animals);
const seen2 = new Set();
const dedupedAnimals2 = allAnimals2.filter(a => !seen2.has(a.animalId) && seen2.add(a.animalId));
const matching30Plus2 = dedupedAnimals2.map(a => {
  const dt = a.residency?.intakeDate ? new Date(a.residency.intakeDate) : null;
  const days = dt ? Math.floor((today2 - dt) / (1000*60*60*24)) : null;
  return {...a, daysOnPetfinder: days, intakeDate: dt ? dt.toISOString().slice(0,10) : null, url: 'https://www.petfinder.com/' + a.publicUrl.url + '/details/'};
}).filter(a => a.daysOnPetfinder !== null && a.daysOnPetfinder > 30);
console.log(JSON.stringify({total:firstPage2.totalCount, fetched: allAnimals2.length, unique: dedupedAnimals2.length, over30: matching30Plus2.length, nullIntake: dedupedAnimals2.filter(a=>!a.residency?.intakeDate).length}, null, 2));
console.log(JSON.stringify(matching30Plus2.slice(0,20).map(a => ({name:a.animalName.trim(), days:a.daysOnPetfinder, intakeDate:a.intakeDate, distance:a.distance, breed:[a.physical?.breed?.primary,a.physical?.breed?.secondary].filter(Boolean).join(' & '), sex:a.physical?.sex, age:a.physical?.age?.label, org:a.organization?.organizationName, url:a.url})), null, 2));

function csvEscape2(v){ const s = String(v ?? ''); return /[",\n]/.test(s) ? '"'+s.replace(/"/g,'""')+'"' : s; }
const fullRows2 = matching30Plus2.map(a => ({
  Name: a.animalName.trim(),
  Age: a.physical?.age?.label || '',
  Sex: a.physical?.sex || '',
  Breed: [a.physical?.breed?.primary,a.physical?.breed?.secondary].filter(Boolean).join(' & '),
  Distance_mi: a.distance,
  Intake_Date: a.intakeDate,
  Days_On_Petfinder: a.daysOnPetfinder,
  Organization: a.organization?.organizationName || '',
  City: a.organization?.organizationCity || '',
  State: a.organization?.organizationState || '',
  URL: a.url
}));
const headers2 = Object.keys(fullRows2[0] || {});
const csv2 = [headers2.join(','), ...fullRows2.map(r => headers2.map(h => csvEscape2(r[h])).join(','))].join('\n');
await fs.writeFile('./artifacts/petfinder_shorthaired_dogs_kids_cats_over30.csv', csv2);
console.log('wrote '+fullRows2.length+' rows');
